To my surprise, after ONE USE my skin was noticeably improved. I woke the next morning and stared in amazement at my face in the mirror -- not only were all my acne spots smaller and MUCH less inflamed than when I'd gone to bed, but my skin had an overall healthy glow to it that is has literally never, ever had before, except perhaps when I was a very young child. The dark red scars all over my cheeks from years' worth of bad breakouts were noticeably lighter. After one use. I was really amazed and couldn't believe the results -- I had to take pictures of myself and compare them to older pictures to be sure I wasn't crazy (I wasn't!). I've now been using AHA Enhanced nightly for about a month. In that time, my skin has been closer to 100% clear than I ever dreamed it could be. It's not totally blemish-free, but the zits I do have are tiny, infrequent, and clear within a day or two (I should note, the supplements I'm taking also have had a noticeable effect, noted before I started using this lotion, so I can't say that my acne success is 100% because of AHA...but it's most definitely helped!) I have also noticed a visible reduction in the fine lines around my eyes. No, this lotion will not make your lines go away entirely, but I have been happy to note that it seems to have turned back the clock on my skin by five years or so. :) I'm hoping thatcontinued use will smooth out the deeper line on my forehead (at least I only have one!) and help prevent more from forming. In addition to using it on my face, I've been using it on my shoulders and back to help clear up my body breakouts. there, too, it's done a remarkable job of reducing the amount of time my spots stick around, reducing redness, and reducing size. I am going to start using the lotion on my entire body because I am enjoying the soft texture and glowing appearance of my face and neck so much. I normally have very sensitive skin and I notice hardly any stinging when using this lotion. It goes away within a couple of minutes. The only drawbacks for me have been the smell -- many people have remarked that this lotion is scent-free, but it does have a noticeably unpleasant odor in my opinion. However, that goes away quickly as the lotion sinks into your skin. This lotion also does such a great job of exfoliating that I've had little flakes form on my face -- something that never ever happened to me before using, since I never could exfoliate well enough before this lotion to make a difference with my acne. But a few quick checks in the mirror daily keep facial flakes from becoming too numerous. I'll be an AHA user for life! This is great stuff!!
